We're looking for brilliant candidates to join our hot Silicon Valley startup, Skin AI LLC. Visit this page to get a sense of what our founders do.
Skin AI uses data science to formulate a completely customized skincare regimen for every user based on results seen by people similar to them. You can check us out at y-ourskin.com. You will be working directly with the two co-founders: Hanh Pham, an M.I.T.-trained data science leader at Pinterest, and Jenny Hanh Nguyen, a serial entrepreneur with multiple successful startups in the beauty space. 






I. PRODUCT MANAGER FOR WEBSITE DEVELOPMENT (FULL-TIME | ONLINE | 3-5 YEARS OF EXPERIENCE | NEGOTIABLE)

1. JOB DESCRIPTION
We are seeking an experienced Product Manager specializing in Website Development, with a minimum of 3 to 5 years of proven expertise in the field. The ideal candidate will have a strong technical background, preferably with experience in eCommerce, to ensure our website's seamless functionality and enhance customer experience.
Position: Product Manager (3 - 5 years of experience)
Location: Online, within Vietnam. 
Employment type: Full-time  -  No Moonlighting allowed, Must be graduated or already finished studies
Package: gross - negotiable
Job Industry: Skincare 
Main Markets: U.S. & Canada. 
2. JOB DUTIES & RESPONSIBILITIES: 
Strategic Planning: Work directly with the founders on website product management and strategy. 
Product Development: Manage the entire lifecycle of customer-facing products, product flow, and feature testing. Ensuring the best experience for customers. 
Performance Monitoring: Monitor website performance metrics, conduct A/B tests, and analyze data to optimize user experience, conversion rates, and overall website effectiveness.
Requirement Analysis: Conduct market research, competitor analysis, and user (customer) feedback analysis to identify enhancement opportunities for website improvements.
Cross-functional Collaboration: Coordinate and collaborate closely with stakeholders, including engineering, design, marketing, and customer support teams, to ensure seamless coordination and alignment of efforts toward the founders' vision. 
3. REQUIREMENTS
MUST HAVE
Fluency in English: A minimum 7.0 IELTS or equivalence. Certificate is required. 
Strong Technical Background with 3 to 5 years of Product Management Experience: Demonstrated track record in product management, preferably in eCommerce or related industries, focusing on website development.
Excellent communication skills with the ability to collaborate effectively with founders and cross-functional teams. 
Analytical Mindset: Proficiency in leveraging data-driven insights and analytics tools to make informed decisions and drive product enhancements.
Can-do attitude: Ability to flourish with minimal guidance, and be proactive with a strong sense of responsibility and proactive work attitude.
Always being prepared, ready for any challenges, and persistent to success with minimal guidance, uncertainty, and ambiguity.
Ability to work flexibly: weekends, flexible hours, and late hours for the US market.
PREFER TO HAVE
Familiarity with SEO, UX/UI principles, and best practices in online merchandising.
7.0+ IELTS or previous studying or living experience in the U.S. are a plus.
Customer-driven mindset: be able to have a strong understanding of customers' references, sympathize with their pain points, and effectively align our products and services to satisfy their expectations. 
Strong passion for Start-up, Marketing, eCommerce, and Skincare.
OTHER REQUIREMENTS 
Personal Laptop.
4. BENEFITS
Standard package: (Gross - negotiable)
Probation: 02 months (100% salary)
Minimum 12 annual leaves, 13th-month salary.

II. CUSTOMER SUPPORT AGENT (FULL-TIME | HA NOI & HYBRID | NO EXPERIENCED REQUIRED | PACKAGE FROM 10.000.000 TO 14.000.000 VND PLUS BONUS)

1. JOB DESCRIPTION
If you're a fresh and energetic graduate who is also self-driven, earnest, and willing to learn & develop a career as a customer support agent in a dynamic and challenging start-up environment, then we want you on our team!
Position: Customer Support Agent (Fresher/Junior - up to 1 year of experience)
Location: Ha Noi / Hybrid - Both offline & online, team meeting offline 2 to 3 times per week in Hanoi, flexible locations.
Employment type: Full-time  -  No Moonlighting allowed, Must be graduated or already finished studies
Package: 10 to 14 million VND plus bonus (gross). 
Job Industry: Skincare. 
Main Markets: U.S. & Canada. 
A DAY IN THE LIFE
After training, possess a strong understanding of the nature of services, products, and customer service operations in a dynamic and intense start-up environment (including multiple e-commerce platforms).
Proactively and promptly engage in customer queries and effectively address their issues/requests with thoughtful and accurate email responses to ensure the highest level of customer satisfaction.

Opportunity to learn in-depth skincare knowledge with our team of skincare experts to become a skincare consultant.

2. REQUIREMENTS
MUST HAVE
Fluency in written English: minimum 7.0 IELTS writing or equivalent (certificate is not required)
Fresh graduate/Junior - up to 1 year of experience
Can-do attitude: Ability to flourish with minimal guidance, and be proactive with a strong sense of responsibility. 
Great attention to detail: strictly follow instructions, and understand the process, platforms & customer experience flow. Modify the existing responses/templates to give customers the best support they need.
A great team player: who is willing to align personal goals with the team's objectives in a positive, collaborative manner while also capable of delivering effective communication and constructive feedback.
Ability to work flexibly: weekends, flexible hours, and late hours for the US market. (No overnight shift). 
Patience and the ability to remain calm in stressful situations.
PREFER TO HAVE
Customer-driven mindset: be able to manage, prioritize, and follow up on customer requests in an organized and actionable manner to achieve the highest level of satisfaction.
Enthusiasm for customer satisfaction, solutions & start-up environment.
Strong passion & knowledge for skincare or experience in the beauty industry is a great plus! 
OTHER REQUIREMENTS 
Personal Laptop.
The cover letter & CV must be in English.

3. BENEFITS

Our AI-powered platform will help clients make smarter marketing decisions such as new ads optimization, new approach for email marketing, smarter budget allocation for the next marketing campaign and much more. Our roots are in data and we love it - itâ€™s where we get to understand different audiences, to experiment, to gain insight and to see how people really engage and respond to ideas.

About the job

COMPANY OVERVIEW

Fuse is an insurtech platform that connects various insurance products from many insurance companies with multiple distribution means, channels, or partners. We deploy the latest cutting edge technology to make insurance easy and affordable for anyone. Our platform support primarily 3 business models, namely Business-To-Agents/Brokers (B2A), Business-To-Customers (B2C), as well as Micro Insurance (B2B2C).

Our Fuse Pro App is tailor-made for B2A business. This App enables anyone to become an independent insurance consultant to act like an expert; to instantly curate the most suitable and best insurance products for their customers. Our B2B2C model supports digital small ticket size insurance products, making insurance affordable for everyone.

Fuse is a brand trusted by channel partners like Tokopedia, Grab, 30+ insurance companies, along with 40,000+ registered partners. Fuse currently generates more than 2.5 million insurance policies each month.

We have more than 400 teammates, with 15 branches, across 4 countries, we strive to be the #1 insurtech platform in SEA and make insurance available for everyone in the region.

AnyMind Group is a technology company that provides a one-stop platform for brands to support production, e-commerce construction, marketing, and logistics. AnyMind Group was founded in April 2016 by Kosuke Sogo and Otohiko Kozutsumi, and has expanded its business to 13 markets and 17 locations worldwide.
We started in the marketing tech industry and expanded our business into influencer marketing, publisher monetization and creator support and management. Now, we are developing and providing software that supports individuals and businesses for brand product planning and manufacturing, e-commerce enablement, marketing, and logistics. With our mission to "make every business borderless", we will continue to remove borders between online and offline, geographical boundaries and industries through the power of data and technology.

What You Will Do

Good at communication/negotiation/presentation skill.
Fluency in spoken and written English


Why You'll Love It

Maido is an AI-powered agency platform that provides smart marketing solutions for SME in Japan and Vietnam. Maido was established in 2019 with the goal of providing marketing solutions for small and medium enterprises using Artificial Intelligence. We believe that the process of marketing should be transparent, with no guesswork. That's why we base everything on data to make decisions. Our AI-powered platform will help clients make smarter marketing decisions such as new ads optimization, new approach for email marketing, smarter budget allocation for the next marketing campaign and much more. POSITION TITLE: SALES & MARKETING INTERN
Maido is seeking a Sales Marketing Intern, who will be largely responsible for the day-to-day execution including responding to customer inquiries, selling marketing packages, and writing various Digital Content. This position is a great match for a second- year student who sets sales/marketing/content as her career journey & wants to step into the world of Digital Transformation. 
You are required to assist in selling social media's packages & creating short/long videos or multi photos to meet campaign's objectives. Therefore, a Sales & Marketing Intern must have experience in using social media platforms (Facebook, Tiktok,..), online apps (Canva, Capcut, VSCOCam, Inshot,..)
